<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;1.01.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As previously disclosed by StepStone Group Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;), the Company established a platform designed to expand access to the private markets for <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap">high-net-worth</span></span> and accredited investors, known as Conversus. Conversus is in an early stage of its lifecycle and, to date, has been loss-making as it has required a net investment from StepStone to facilitate development of its capabilities and growth of its client base. At the establishment of the platform, the Conversus management team, through an entity named Conversus Holdings LLC (&#8220;CH&#8221;), were provided an ability to acquire the platform from StepStone in exchange for an amount which would have provided StepStone a return of its initial investment plus an equity return. The Company is today announcing the entering into of new arrangements, including the Option Agreement attached hereto as Exhibit 10.1 (the &#8220;Option Agreement&#8221;), which arrangements are intended to update the legacy Conversus compensation structure to better incentivize the Conversus team to grow the platform, while ensuring the platform will remain part of StepStone going forward. In connection with the announcement, the Conversus platform and its associated retail funds are expected to be rebranded as StepStone Private Wealth. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The summary below of the Option Agreement is a summary only and the full terms of the Option Agreement are incorporated by reference herein. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As part of the new arrangements, the team will receive a profits interest (the &#8220;Profits Interest&#8221;) in StepStone Conversus LLC (to be renamed StepStone Group Private Wealth LLC). Under the Option Agreement, (i)&#160;StepStone has the right to acquire the Profits Interest at the end of any fiscal quarter after June&#160;30, 2027, in exchange for payment of a call price and (ii)&#160;CH has the right to put the Profits Interest to StepStone on June&#160;30, 2026, September&#160;30, 2026, December&#160;31, 2026, March&#160;31, 2027 or June&#160;30, 2027 or at the end of any fiscal quarter after June&#160;30, 2027, in exchange for payment of a put price. The applicable call or put price is, in certain circumstances, subject to an earnout or earndown. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The call or put price will be payable in cash unless the Company elects to pay a portion of the consideration in units of StepStone Group LP (&#8220;SSG Units&#8221;), each to be exchangeable into shares of the Company&#8217;s Class&#160;A Common Stock, and, in either case, rights under one or more tax receivable agreements. The Company has the right, but not the obligation, to pay up to 75% of the consideration in SSG Units. If the Company does elect to issue SSG Units, 70% of such SSG Units will be subject to a <span style="white-space:nowrap">lock-up,</span> with <span style="white-space:nowrap">one-third</span> of the units released from the lockup on each of the first, second and third anniversaries after issuance. If the Company determines that the SSG Units to be issued pursuant to the Option Agreement would represent more than 20% of the Company&#8217;s outstanding shares of Class&#160;A Common Stock at the time of issuance, it would expect to obtain shareholder approval of such issuances prior to the closing of the applicable call or put. J.P. Morgan Securities LLC acted as financial advisor to the Company. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A related FAQ is made available on the Company&#8217;s website at: https://shareholders.stepstonegroup.com/. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.03.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an <span style="white-space:nowrap">Off-Balance</span> Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information set forth in Item 1.01 is incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 10.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OPTION AGREEMENT </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This
<B>OPTION AGREEMENT </B>(this &#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;), dated as of November&nbsp;2, 2022 (the &#147;<U>Effective Date</U>&#148;), is entered into between Conversus Holdings LLC, a North Carolina limited liability company
(&#147;<U>CH</U>&#148;), StepStone Group LP, a Delaware limited partnership (&#147;<U>StepStone</U>&#148;), StepStone Group Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U>STEP</U>&#148; and, together with StepStone, the &#147;<U>Purchasers</U>&#148;) and
StepStone Conversus LLC, to be renamed as StepStone Group Private Wealth LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (the &#147;<U>Adviser</U>&#148; or the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148; and, together with CH, StepStone, and STEP, each a
&#147;<U>Party</U>&#148; and together the &#147;<U>Parties</U>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RECITALS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, StepStone owns one hundred percent (100%) of the issued and outstanding limited liability company interests in the Adviser; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, simultaneously with this Agreement, and effective as of the Effective Date, various of the Parties will enter into (i)&nbsp;the
Binding Memorandum of Understanding, (ii)&nbsp;the Second Amended and Restated Limited Liability Company Agreement of the Company (the &#147;<U>Adviser LLC Agreement</U>&#148;), (iii) the Services Agreement, and (iv)&nbsp;the Loan and Security
Agreement and related documents (the &#147;<U>Loan Documents</U>&#148; and collectively, the &#147;<U>2022 Conversus-Related Agreements</U>&#148;); </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Adviser intends to issue (i)&nbsp;to CH a new class of limited liability company interests (the &#147;<U>Profits
Interest</U>&#148;) denominated as Class&nbsp;B units, and (ii)&nbsp;to HC Equity Partners LLC (&#147;<U>HC</U>&#148;), a North Carolina limited liability company, a new class of limited liability company interests denominated as Class&nbsp;C units,
all as contemplated by the Adviser LLC Agreement; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, this Agreement is entered into to (i)&nbsp;provide CH with the right to
require STEP and StepStone, as more fully described below, to purchase such Profits Interest, and (ii)&nbsp;provide StepStone with a right to purchase such Profits Interest, in each case on the respective terms set forth herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AGREEMENT </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NOW,
THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing and the mutual covenants and agreements herein contained, and intending to be legally bound hereby, the Parties agree as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1. <U>Put and Call Option</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) During the period commencing April&nbsp;1, 2026 and on or prior to June&nbsp;30, 2027 (the &#147;<U>Put Only Period</U>&#148;), or on or
after July&nbsp;1, 2027 (the &#147;<U>Put/Call Option Period</U>&#148;), CH shall have the right, but not the obligation, to deliver an irrevocable written notice of election to the Purchasers (the &#147;<U>Put Notice</U>&#148;, and the transaction
resulting from the Put Notice, the &#147;<U>Put</U>&#148;) to initiate the purchase by the Purchasers from CH of all or a portion of the Profits Interest (as specified in the applicable Put Notice, the &#147;<U>Put Interest</U>&#148;) on the terms
and subject to the conditions set forth in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;2</B>. Any portion of the Profits Interest not purchased as of any given date that remains subject to a Put or a Call (as defined below) shall be referred to herein as the
&#147;<U>Outstanding </U><U>Profits Interest.</U>&#148; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) During the Put/Call Option Period, the Purchasers shall have the right, but not the
obligation, to deliver an irrevocable written notice of election to CH (the &#147;<U>Call Notice</U>,&#148; and the transaction resulting from the Call Notice, the &#147;<U>Call</U>&#148;), to initiate the purchase by the Purchasers from CH of not
less than all of the Outstanding Profits Interest (as specified in the applicable Call Notice, the &#147;<U>Call Interest</U>&#148;) on the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;3</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) For purposes of this Agreement, the term &#147;<U>Acquired Interest</U>&#148; shall refer to such portion of the Profits Interest (either
the Put Interest, subject to the Put Cutback provided in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;2(d)</B>, or the Call Interest) actually sold by CH and acquired by Purchasers pursuant to a Put or Call. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. <U>Put Option Exercise</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) CH may deliver up to two Put Notices, subject to the conditions below, each of which must specify a date that is the last day of the
StepStone fiscal quarter during which the Put Notice is made (the date so specified, the &#147;<U>Put Determination Date</U>&#148;). If a Put Notice is delivered during the Put Only Period, the Put Determination Date must be one of June&nbsp;30,
2026, September&nbsp;30, 2026, December&nbsp;31, 2026, March&nbsp;31, 2027 or June&nbsp;30, 2027 &#150; the fiscal <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">quarter-end</FONT> immediately following the Put Notice. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The first Put Notice must specify the portion of the Profits Interest to be purchased, which must not be less than (i)&nbsp;eighty percent
(80%) of the Profits Interest, if the Put Notice is delivered during the Put Only Period and (ii)&nbsp;one hundred percent (100%) of the Profits Interest, if the Put Notice is delivered during the Put/Call Option Period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) The second Put Notice, if any, shall require the Purchasers to acquire all the Outstanding Profits Interest. Unless StepStone exercises
its Put Cutback right as described in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;2(d)</B>, the Put Determination Date for the second Put Notice may not be earlier than the last day of the third fiscal quarter after the Put Determination Date for the first Put
Notice. For example, if CH delivers a Put Notice for 80% with respect to a June&nbsp;30, 2026 Put Determination Date, then CH may not deliver a Put Notice for the Outstanding Profits Interest until January&nbsp;1, 2027, the first day of the quarter
ending March&nbsp;31, 2027. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) If the first Put Notice is delivered during the Put Only Period and specifies that it is with respect to
more than eighty percent (80%) of the Profits Interest, then StepStone may, by notice to CH to be provided no later than ten (10)&nbsp;days after StepStone&#146;s receipt of the first Put Notice, reduce the amount of Profits Interest to be Put to
not less than eighty percent (80%) (such reduction, a &#147;<U>Put Cutback</U>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) Notwithstanding the foregoing provisions of
this <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;2</B>, StepStone may Call the Outstanding Profits Interest at any time after the beginning of the Put/Call Option Period pursuant to <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;3</B>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">3. <U>Call Option Exercise</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) Subject to the conditions herein, the Purchasers may deliver a Call Notice, which Call Notice must specify a date that is the last day of
the StepStone fiscal quarter during which the Call Notice is made (and no earlier than September&nbsp;30, 2027 (the date so specified, the &#147;<U>Call Determination Date</U>,&#148; and any Call Determination Date or Put Determination Date being a
&#147;<U>Determination Date</U>&#148;)). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The Call Notice, if any, shall require the Purchasers to acquire not less than all of the
Outstanding Profits Interest. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">4. <U>Option Closing and Effective Dates</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) <U>Net Purchase Price Determination</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) The Net Purchase Price for the Acquired Interest, excluding the portion of the Net Purchase Price that is attributable to
Total Current Year Incentive Fees, shall be jointly determined by CH and StepStone promptly, and no more than five Business Days, following the filing of STEP&#146;s Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> or
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K,</FONT> as applicable, with respect to the fiscal quarter ending on the Determination Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) The Net Purchase Price for the Acquired Interest that is attributable to Total Current Year Incentive Fees shall be
jointly determined by CH and StepStone promptly and no more than thirty (30)&nbsp;days following payment by the relevant Incentive Fee Fund(s) of the Incentive Fees in respect of the Latest Incentive Fee Period End. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) <U>Closing Dates</U>. Each purchase and sale of an Acquired Interest (the &#147;<U>Closing</U>&#148;) shall, subject to the satisfaction
of all the conditions in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(d)</B>, take place on a Business Day (each such date, a &#147;<U>Closing Date</U>&#148;) reasonably agreed by the Parties, not later than ten (10)&nbsp;Business Days after the determination of
the Net Purchase Price, excluding the portion of the Net Purchase Price that is attributable to Total Current Year Incentive Fees, in accordance with <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(a)(i)</B>. As contemplated in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(a),
</B>payment of the Net Purchase Price attributable to each Acquired Interest will occur in two installments but, for the avoidance of doubt and subject to the satisfaction of all the conditions in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(d),</B> the
effective date of the transfer of the Acquired Interest from CH to the Purchasers and the issuance of SSG Units (as defined below) by StepStone to CH in respect of the Acquired Interest shall be the applicable Determination Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) <U>Conditions to Closing and Closing</U>. The respective obligations of the Purchasers and CH to consummate any sale and purchase under
this Agreement will be subject to the satisfaction, as of the applicable Closing Date, of the following conditions: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i)
there is no pending or threatened action or proceeding by or before any court or other governmental body or governmental agency that seeks to restrain, prohibit or invalidate the transactions contemplated hereby; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) the representations and warranties provided by the Other Parties (as defined below) under the 2022 Conversus-Related
Agreements are true and accurate in all material respects; and </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) the Other Parties have complied in all material respects with the 2022
Conversus-Related Agreements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) <U>Closing</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) At each Closing, (i)&nbsp;CH shall assign (x)&nbsp;to STEP that portion of the Acquired Interest corresponding to the
amount of cash paid by STEP, as elected by the Purchasers pursuant to <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(f)</B>, relative to the Net Purchase Price for the Acquired Interest, and (y)&nbsp;to StepStone, the remainder of the Acquired Interest,
(ii)&nbsp;STEP shall execute and deliver to CH the TRAs referred to in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;8</B> applicable to such Acquired Interest, and (iii)&nbsp;the Purchasers shall deliver an amount of cash and SSG Units equal to the Net Purchase
Price for such Acquired Interest, excluding the portion of the Net Purchase Price that attributable to Total Current Year Incentive Fees, as more specifically prescribed in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(f)</B>. As of such Closing Date, CH shall
represent to the Purchasers that the Acquired Interest was at all times held legally and beneficially by CH free and clear of all liens and other encumbrances, other that liens arising under the Loan Documents, and that StepStone shall acquire valid
title to the Acquired Interest. CH shall account to the Purchasers for any distributions made to it between the Determination Date and the Closing Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) Promptly, and in any event no later than five (5)&nbsp;Business Days after the determination and payment described in
<B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(a)(ii)</B>,<B> </B>the Purchasers shall deliver an amount of cash and SSG Units equal to the portion of the Net Purchase Price for such Acquired Interest that is attributable to Total Current Year Incentive Fees as
more specifically prescribed in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(f)</B>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) <U>Escrow</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Ten percent (10%) of the Net Purchase Price consideration payable in connection with any Put exercised during the Put Only
Period shall be delivered into an escrow account to provide for and protect Purchasers with respect to a potential Earndown adjustment pursuant to <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5</B>; <I>provided</I>, that all interest, dividends, distributions,
income, capital gains and other amounts earned on such consideration deposited with the escrow agent (regardless of form) shall be the property of CH. For the avoidance of doubt, the cash and SSG Units (as defined below) payable in connection with
any Put during the Put Only Period shall be placed into escrow <I>pro rata</I> based on the entire amount of consideration payable under such Put; <I>provided</I>, <I>further</I> that upon satisfaction of any Earnout or Earndown pursuant to
<B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5(e)</B> or <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5(f)</B>, respectively, all Net Purchase Price consideration remaining in escrow for the relevant Put shall be released to CH within five (5)&nbsp;Business Days. This escrow
requirement shall not apply in the event of a Call or a Put exercised during the Put/Call Option Period. The escrow account shall be established with a bank selected by, and on terms reasonably acceptable to, the Board (as defined in the Adviser LLC
Agreement). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) None of the SSG Units described in clause (i)&nbsp;of <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(f)</B> (i.e. the
unrestricted SSG Units) shall be placed into the aforesaid escrow account, and any SSG Units delivered into escrow pursuant to this <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(e)</B> will be considered &#147;issued&#148; as of the applicable Closing Date for
purposes of the transfer restrictions described in <B>Section </B><B>4(f)</B>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) <U>Form of Payment; Transfer Restrictions</U>. Payment of the Net Purchase Price with
respect to each Acquired Interest will be made by STEP in cash or, at StepStone&#146;s sole election, up to 75% of the Net Purchase Price may be paid in the form of StepStone limited partnership units (&#147;<U>SSG Units</U>&#148;). Each such SSG
Unit shall have no less favorable economic terms than the Class&nbsp;A, Class&nbsp;B and Class&nbsp;C StepStone limited partnership units, including as to priority of distributions and anti-dilution protection, and shall be exchangeable into one
share of Common Stock (as defined below), such exchanges to be subject to the generally applicable terms of (i)&nbsp;StepStone&#146;s then-current partnership agreement, (ii)&nbsp;the STEP exchange agreement applicable to existing StepStone limited
partnership units and (iii)&nbsp;STEP&#146;s insider trading policy, none of which shall be amended by StepStone or STEP in a manner that by its terms treats CH differently than other holders of SSG Units or Common Stock generally (other than STEP
in its capacity as holder of SSG Units), with the remaining portion of the Net Purchase Price payable in cash by STEP. For such purpose, each SSG Unit will be deemed to have a value equal to the arithmetic average of the Daily VWAP for the ten
(10)&nbsp;consecutive Trading Days ending on, and including, the Determination Date. The Parties intend that any SSG Units received by CH in exchange for Acquired Interests pursuant to this Section shall be received pursuant to Section&nbsp;721 of
the Code to the extent permitted by applicable law at the time that such Units are received.&nbsp;No SSG Units will be subject to vesting. However, the SSG Units (and any Common Stock issued upon exchange thereof) will be subject to the following
contractual transfer restrictions: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) 30% of the SSG Units initially issued (and the Common Stock issuable in exchange
for such SSG Units) on the applicable Closing Date will not be subject to any contractual transfer restriction; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) 23.3%
of the SSG Units initially issued (and the Common Stock issuable in exchange for such SSG Units) on the applicable Closing Date may not be transferred until the first anniversary of the Determination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) 23.4% of the SSG Units initially issued (and the Common Stock issuable in exchange for such SSG Units) on the applicable
Closing Date may not be transferred until the second anniversary of the Determination Date; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) 23.3% of the SSG Units
initially issued (and the Common Stock issuable in exchange for such SSG Units) on the applicable Closing Date may not be transferred until the third anniversary of the Determination Date; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>provided</I>, <I>however</I>, that if the total value of SSG Units issued in consideration of the Acquired Interest is less than the greater of (x)
$25&nbsp;million or (y)&nbsp;the product of (1)&nbsp;the average dollar value of the daily trading volume using the ten (10)&nbsp;consecutive Trading Days ending on, and including, the second Trading Day prior to the applicable Closing Date
<I>multiplied by</I> (2)&nbsp;two (such condition being met, the &#147;<U>Materiality Benchmark</U>&#148;), then the foregoing transfer restrictions in this <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(f) </B>will not apply. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">5 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) <U>Transfer Restrictions on </U><U>Earnout</U><U> Units</U>. Any SSG Units issued
pursuant to an Earnout (as defined below) under <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5</B> or an Additional Earnout (as defined below) under <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;6</B> will be subject to transfer restrictions in accordance with the schedule
provided in clauses (f)(i) to (f)(iv) above, as determined from the Determination Date in respect of the Acquired Interest to which such Earnout or Addditional Earnout relates; <I>provided</I>, <I>however</I>, that if the Materiality Benchmark is
not exceeded with respect to the SSG Units previously issued to CH and such SSG Units issued pursuant to an Earnout or an Additional Earnout, then such transfer restrictions will not apply. For example, if SSG Units are issued pursuant to an Earnout
or an Additional Earnout that relates to a Put having a Put Determination Date of June&nbsp;30, 2026, 53.3% of such SSG Units will not be subject to any contractual transfer restriction when issued, 23.4% of such SSG Units may not be transferred
until June&nbsp;30, 2028 and 23.3% of such SSG Units may not be transferred until June&nbsp;30, 2029. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">5.
<U>Earnout</U><U>/</U><U>Earndown</U><U> Adjustments</U>. The Net Purchase Price with respect to each Acquired Interest will be subject to a positive adjustment (an &#147;<U>Earnout</U>&#148;) in the manner set forth below for incremental growth in <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Earnings for the twelve months ended on the first anniversary of the Determination Date (the &#147;<U>Adjustment Determination Date</U>&#148;), resulting from the impact of positive Net Capital Flows (as
defined below) with regard to the Funds during such twelve months. If CH exercises its Put during the Put Only Period, then the Net Purchase Price would also be subject to a negative adjustment (an &#147;<U>Earndown</U>&#148;) in the manner set
forth below for any incremental decline in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Earnings resulting from the impact of negative Net Capital Flows during such twelve months. For the avoidance of doubt, (x)&nbsp;a Put during the Put Only
Period for all or less than all of the Profits Interest is subject to the Earnout and Earndown, as applicable, and (y)&nbsp;a Put or Call during the Put/Call Option Period is not subject to an Earndown. In determining the amount of any such
adjustment: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) The adjustment will utilize the same Purchase Multiple as applied to reach the original Gross Purchase Price applicable
to the Acquired Interest. By way of example, if the original Purchase Multiple were 15x, the Earnout or Earndown calculation would use the same 15x. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) Except as set forth in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5(c)</B>, the principles used to calculate the components used to determine the
Earnout or Earndown and the dates for making determinations will be the same principles and dates used to calculate the Net Purchase Price (as such dates will be rolled forward one year to the extent contemplated by this
<B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5</B>). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) Any Earnout or Earndown will be calculated in the manner set forth in this
<B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5(c), </B>as illustrated in <U>Schedule A</U>. The Parties intend that the methodology reflect the cumulative impact of actual monthly Net Capital Flows for each Fund for each of the twelve months ending on the
applicable Adjustment Determination Date, determined as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) For each Fund, actual cumulative Net Capital Flows
will be <I>multiplied</I> by the applicable Management Fee Rates for the relevant twelve months, in the same manner as applied for purposes of determining &#147;Basic ANI&#148; to calculate the Gross Purchase Price. The sum of such products for all
twelve months for all Funds shall constitute the &#147;<U>Total Incremental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Revenue</U>&#148; for such period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) The total Incremental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Revenue <U>multiplied</U> by the Cumulative FRE
Margin (as defined below) will yield the &#147;<U>Total Pre-Tax Incremental FRE</U>.&#148; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) Total Pre-Tax Incremental FRE shall then be <I>reduced by</I> taxes at
STEP&#146;s blended statutory rate. The resulting difference (the &#147;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">After-Tax</FONT> Incremental FRE</U>&#148;) shall then be <I>multiplied</I> by the same Purchase Multiple applied to determine the Gross
Purchase Price for the Acquired Interest, and then further multipled by the Applicable Sales Percentage for such Acquired Interest, to determine any Earnout adjustment with respect to such Acquired Interest, subject to Section&nbsp;5(d) below. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) In the case of a Put during the Put Only Period, any Earndown adjustment shall be determined in the same manner and using
the same principles as an Earnout adjustment, except that the amount determined pursuant to the foregoing formula prior to the reduction of taxes will be positively adjusted for the tax savings resulting from lower
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Earnings at STEP&#146;s blended statutory rate, thereby reducing the amount of the Earndown that would have been the case without such adjustment. For the avoidance of doubt, the Earnout or
Earndown adjustments shall exclude Incentive Fees and any effect portfolio valuation changes may have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Earnings. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) Any Earnout or Earndown adjustment will be limited to ten percent (10%) of the original Net Purchase Price applicable to the Acquired
Interest but will remain subject to the Additional Earnout described in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;6</B> below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) Any additional
payment made to CH pursuant to an Earnout will be paid using the same form of consideration, and provided by the relevant Purchaser, as was used to pay the original Net Purchase Price no later than ten (10)&nbsp;days after the determination of the
Earnout adjustment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) Any SSG Units issued as an Earnout shall not be subject to vesting but will be subject to contractual transfer
restrictions as set forth in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(f)</B>, as modified by <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(g)</B>. The Parties intend that any SSG Units received by CH pursuant to this Section shall be received pursuant to Section&nbsp;721
of the Code to the extent permitted under applicable law at the time that such Units are received. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) Any payment in respect of an
Earndown shall be paid on the same schedule as provided for payment of an Earnout in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5(e)</B>, with such payment to be made out of the escrow account described in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(e)(</B><B>i</B><B>)</B>
hereof. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">6. <U>Additional </U><U>Earnout</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) If (i)&nbsp;the Purchase Multiple with respect to an Acquired Interest is 15x or less and (ii)&nbsp;actual Basic ANI for the six month
period ending on the applicable Determination Date is at least 90% of the projected Basic ANI for the same six month period in the July 2022 management forecast as set forth in <U>Schedule B</U> hereto, then CH will have the opportunity to receive
an additional positive adjustment (an &#147;<U>Additional Earnout</U>&#148;); <I>provided </I>that, if the Determination Date is after March&nbsp;31, 2027 (the final period in the forecast), then the comparison will be the Adviser&#146;s actual
Basic ANI for the last six months of its fiscal year ending March&nbsp;31, 2027, relative to the Basic ANI shown in the forecast for the last six months of the fiscal year ending March&nbsp;31, 2027. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The Additional Earnout applicable to the Acquired Interest will be reflected as an
upward adjustment to the ten percent (10%) of Net Purchase Price limitation on the Earnout set forth in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5(d)</B>, by adding the Additional Earnout Percentage to such limitation. For purposes of this
<B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;6</B>, &#147;<U>Additional Earnout Percentage</U>&#148; means (i)&nbsp;the lesser of 5% and (ii) (x) 50% multiplied by (y)&nbsp;the percentage points, or fractions thereof, by which actual Basic ANI relative to the
applicable management forecast, using the same principles used in the forecast, exceeds 90%. For example, if Basic ANI is 95% of management&#146;s forecast for the relevant period, then the Additional Earnout Percentage will be 2.5% and if Basic ANI
is greater than or equal to 100% of management&#146;s forecast for the relevant period, then the Additional Earnout Percentage will be 5.0% of the Net Purchase Price. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) The Additional Earnout with respect to each Acquired Interest will be calculated and paid in the same manner as the Earnout with respect
to such Acquired Interest set forth in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;5</B>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) Any Additional Earnout payment made to CH pursuant to an
Additional Earnout will be paid using the same form of consideration, and provided by the relevant Purchaser, as was used to pay the original Net Purchase Price. Any SSG Units issued as an Additional Earnout shall not be subject to vesting but will
be subject to contractual transfer restrictions as set forth in <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(f)</B>, as qualified by <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;4(g)</B>. The Parties intend that any SSG Units received by CH pursuant to this Section shall be
received pursuant to Section&nbsp;721 of the Code to the extent permitted under applicable law at the time such Units are received. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">7.
<U>Definitions</U>. In addition to other defined terms set forth in this Agreement, which shall apply for all purposes of this Agreement, the following terms shall have the following meanings ascribed thereto: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) &#147;<U>Accounting Firm</U>&#148; shall mean BDO USA, LLP; provided, however, if BDO USA, LLP has provided any material accounting
services to StepStone or CH, or their controlling persons, during the three-year period prior to their selection to serve as the expert for a dispute pursuant to <B>Section</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;12(j)</B>, or are otherwise required to be independent,
then the Accounting Firm shall be Grant Thornton LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) &#147;<U>Actual Distribution Costs</U>&#148; means, with respect to any period,
internal and external commissions, distribution personnel guarantees, costs paid to third parties, including placement fees, required due diligence fees or required conference sponsorships as the same are expensed under generally accepted accounting
standards (GAAP) for such period. With effect from the Effective Date, Actual Distribution Costs shall be amortized as an expense on a straight-line basis over four years for the purpose of determining Adviser ANI, and such amount for such period
will be known as &#147;<U>Amortized Distribution Costs</U>.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) &#147;<U>Adjusted Adviser ANI</U>&#148; means, with respect to any
period, the sum of (without duplication): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Adviser ANI; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) <I>minus</I> Incentive Fees (whether realized or unrealized); and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) <I>plus</I> (to the extent taken into account to reduce Adviser ANI) performance
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">fee-related</FONT> compensation. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">By way of example, a calculation of Adviser ANI and Adjusted Adviser ANI for the LTM ended June&nbsp;30,
2022 is set forth in <U>Schedule C</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) &#147;<U>Adviser ANI</U>&#148; means, with respect to any period, the sum of (without
duplication): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) Basic ANI; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) <I>minus</I> fees in respect of any SSG balance sheet investments in the Adviser&#146;s products; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) <I>minus</I> Legacy HNW Feeder <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-ups;</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) <I>plus </I>Actual Distribution Costs; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(v) <I>minus </I>Amortized Distribution Costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) &#147;<U>Applicable Sale Percentage</U>&#148; means, with respect to the exercise of any Put or Call under this Agreement, the portion,
expressed as a percentage, of the Acquired Interest relative to the entire Profits Interest. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) &#147;<U>Basic ANI</U>&#148; means, with
respect to the Adviser and any period, the sum of (without duplication): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) net management and advisory fees; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) <I>plus </I>Incentive Fees; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) <I>plus </I>realized investment income; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) <I>plus </I>interest income; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(v) <I>plus </I>other income; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(vi) <I>minus </I>realized performance <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">fee-related</FONT> compensation; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(vii) <I>minus </I>generally recurring operating expenses (including equity-based compensation and Actual Distribution Costs);
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(viii) <I>plus </I>charges associated with acquisitions and corporate transactions, contract terminations and employee
severance; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ix) <I>plus </I>amortization of intangibles; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(x) <I>minus </I>interest expense; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(xi) <I>minus </I>other loss </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">as calculated using the principles and methodology applied by STEP in its periodic reports filed with the
Securities and Exchange Commission. By way of example, a calculation of Basic ANI for the LTM ended June&nbsp;30, 2022 is set forth in <U>Schedule C</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) &#147;<U>Business Day</U>&#148; means a day determined by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission to be a business day. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(h) &#147;<U>Code</U>&#148; means the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended from time to time (or any corresponding provisions of
succeeding law). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) &#147;<U>Common Stock</U>&#148; means the Class&nbsp;A common stock of STEP. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(j) &#147;<U>Cumulative FRE Margin</U>&#148; means, with respect to all Funds, the ratio, expressed as a percentage, that (a)&nbsp;the actual <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Earnings for the twelve months ending on the applicable Adjustment Determination Date, bears to (b)&nbsp;the actual <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Revenues for the twelve months
ending on the applicable Adjustment Determination Date, as reflected on Adviser&#146;s financial statements; <U>provided that</U>, for purposes of this definition, Incentive Fees are excluded from revenue and taxes are not deducted. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(k) &#147;<U>Current Year Incentive Fees</U>&#148; means, in respect of any Incentive Fee Fund, the Adviser&#146;s Incentive Fees for the
Incentive Fee Year in which the Determination Date falls. For example, if an Incentive Fee Fund calculates its Incentive Fees on the basis of the 12 months ended June&nbsp;30, and the Determination Date was September&nbsp;30, 2027, then the Current
Year Incentive Fees would be such fees for the Incentive Fee Year ended June&nbsp;30, 2028. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(l) &#147;<U>Daily VWAP</U>&#148; means the

scheduled open of trading until the scheduled close of trading of the primary trading session on such Trading Day (or if such volume-weighted average price is unavailable, the market value of one share of the Common Stock on such Trading Day
determined, using a volume-weighted average method, by a nationally recognized independent investment banking firm retained for this purpose by the Company). The &#147;Daily VWAP&#148; shall be determined without regard to after-hours trading or any
other trading outside of the regular trading session trading hours. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(m) &#147;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT>
Earnings</U>&#148; means, with respect to each Fund, and determined on a monthly basis, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Revenue less applicable expenses as reported on Adviser&#146;s financial statements and calculated on a
consistent basis. For the avoidance of doubt, taxes are not an expense for purposes of determining <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Earnings. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(n) &#147;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Fee-Related</FONT> Revenue</U>&#148; means, with respect to each Fund, the amount calculated on

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(o) &#147;<U>Fund</U>&#148; means any fund or similar vehicle managed or advised by Adviser.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(p) &#147;<U>Gross Purchase Price</U>&#148; means, in respect of any Acquired Interest, an amount equal to the product of: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) the sum of (1)&nbsp;two times the Adjusted Adviser ANI for the six months ending on the applicable Determination Date
<I>plus </I>(2)&nbsp;sixty percent (60%) of the Total Current Year Incentive Fees<I> plus</I> forty percent (40%) of the Total Prior Year Incentive Fees with respect to each Incentive Fee Fund that pays Incentive Fees on an annual basis plus (3)
100% of Total Prior Year Incentive Fees with respect to each Incentive Fee Fund that pays Incentive Fees on a quarterly basis; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) <I>minus</I><I> </I>an amount equal to taxes on such sum at STEP&#146;s blended statutory rate at the time of the
applicable Determination Date; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii) <I>multiplied</I> by the Applicable Sale Percentage; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv) <I>multiplied by </I>the applicable Purchase Multiple. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the avoidance of doubt, to the extent that there is a subsequent payment relating to Total Current Year Incentive Fees pursuant to

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(dd) &#147;<U>Peer Median Multiple</U>&#148; means the median share price multiple of the
companies in the Peer Set, using the reported adjusted net income of the relevant companies in the Peer Set for the LTM ending as of the applicable Determination Date, generally calculated in the same manner as the SSG Multiple. An agreed example of
the calculation of the Peer Median Multiple is attached as <U>Schedule E</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ee) &#147;<U>Peer Set</U>&#148; means the U.S.-listed
alternative asset managers set forth in <U>Schedule F</U> from time to time, each having (i)&nbsp;substantial activity in more than one private market asset class, (ii)&nbsp;a market capitalization of at least $1.5&nbsp;billion and
(iii)&nbsp;coverage by three or more equity research analysts. The Parties shall review the Peer Set annually and use commercially reasonable efforts to update the Peer Set in good faith. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ff) &#147;<U>Percentage Factor</U>&#148;<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP>means (i)&nbsp;if the SSG Multiple is equal to
or greater than 20x, 70% and (ii)&nbsp;if the SSG Multiple is less than 20x, the sum of (A) 70% <I>plus</I> (B)&nbsp;an amount of percentage points, not to exceed thirty (30)&nbsp;percentage points, equal to (x)&nbsp;the difference of 20x
<I>minus</I> the SSG Multiple (expressed as a multiple of &#147;x&#148;) <I>multiplied by</I> (y)&nbsp;two. For example, if the SSG Multiple is 21x, the Percentage Factor shall equal 70%; if the SSG Multiple is 19x, the Percentage Factor shall equal
72%; and if the SSG Multiple is 18.25x, the Percentage Factor shall equal 73.5%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(gg) &#147;<U>Prior Year Incentive Fees</U>&#148; means,
in respect of any Incentive Fee Fund that pays Incentive Fees on an annual basis, the Adviser&#146;s Incentive Fees for the Incentive Fee Year immediately preceding the Incentive Fee Year in which the Determination Date falls; <U>provided that</U>,
in respect of any Incentive Fee Fund that calculates Incentive Fees quarterly, it shall mean the Adviser&#146;s Incentive Fees for the four prior quarters ending on the Determination Date. For example, if an Incentive Fee Fund calculates its
Incentive Fees on the basis of the 12 months ended June&nbsp;30, and the Determination Date was September&nbsp;30, 2027, then the Prior Year Incentive Fees would be such fees for the twelve month period ended June&nbsp;30, 2027. For the avoidance of
doubt, if an Incentive Fee Fund charges Incentive Fees quarterly, and the Determination Date is September&nbsp;30, 2027, then the Prior Year Incentive Fees for such Fund would be the sum of any amounts for quarters ending December&nbsp;31, 2026,
March 31, 2027, June&nbsp;30, 2027 and September&nbsp;30, 2027. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(hh) &#147;<U>Purchase Multiple</U>&#148; means: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) if the SSG Multiple is less than 80% of the Peer Median Multiple, the Purchase Multiple is the lesser of (A) 20x and (B)
95% of the SSG Multiple; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) if the SSG Multiple is equal to or greater than 80% of the Peer Median Multiple, then
the Purchase Multiple is the lesser of (A) 20x and (B)&nbsp;the product of (1)&nbsp;the Percentage Factor <I>multiplied by</I> (2)&nbsp;the SSG Multiple. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii) &#147;<U>Reference Date</U>&#148; means October&nbsp;31, 2022<I>.</I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(jj) &#147;<U>Reference Date Net Investment Amount</U>&#148; means $18,638,153, being the amount agreed to have been invested in the Adviser
by SSG as of the Reference Date. The Parties </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
acknowledge and agree that the Reference Date Net Investment Amount is an estimate as of the Effective Date, and that any required adjustments to such amount to account for actual expenses
incurred prior to the Reference Date shall be added to or deducted from the Net Investment Amount, as applicable. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(kk) &#147;<U>Shared

finance, facilities and other services as reasonably requested by the Company and approved in the Company&#146;s annual budget and operating plan. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ll) &#147;<U>SSG Multiple</U>&#148; means the quotient, determined as of a Determination Date, of (A)&nbsp;the arithmetic average of the
Daily VWAP for the ten (10)&nbsp;consecutive Trading Days ending on, and including, the Determination Date, <I>divided</I> by (B)&nbsp;the SSG Reported ANI over the LTM ending on the Determination Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(mm) &#147;<U>SSG Reported ANI</U>&#148; means, with respect to any period, the adjusted net income of SSG, as publicly reported for such
period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(nn) &#147;<U>Total Current Year Incentive Fees</U>&#148; means an amount, determined promptly following the Latest Incentive Fee
Period End after the relevant Determination Date with respect to an Acquired Interest, equal to the sum for all Current Year Incentive Fees for all Incentive Fee Funds whose Incentive Fund Period includes the Determination Date for such Acquired
Interest, calculated in accordance with the definition of Current Year Incentive Fees; <U>provided, however</U>, with respect to any Incentive Fee Fund (x)&nbsp;that calculates its Incentive Fees on a 12 month basis but (y)&nbsp;whose Incentive Fund
Year ending prior to the Determination Date is not a full <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-months</FONT> following the launch of such Incentive Fee Fund, the Current Year Incentive Fees for such Incentive Fee Fund will be doubled for purposes of
calculating the Total Current Year Incentive Fees (and the Incentive Fees for such prior Incentive Fund Year will be disregarded). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(oo)
&#147;<U>Total Prior Year Incentive Fees</U>&#148; means an amount, determined as of the Determination Date with respect to an Acquired Interest, equal to the sum of all Prior Year Incentive Fees for all Incentive Fee Funds calculated in accordance
with the definition of Prior Year Incentive Fees in respect of such Acquired Interest; <I>provided, however</I>, with respect to any Incentive Fee Fund (x)&nbsp;that calculates its Incentive Fees on a 12 month basis but (y)&nbsp;whose Incentive Fund
Year ending prior to the Determination Date is not a full <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-months</FONT> following the launch of such Incentive Fee Fund, the Prior Year Incentive Fees for such Incentive Fee Fund will be excluded for purposes of
calculating the Total Prior Year Incentive Fees. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(pp) &#147;<U>Trading Day</U>&#148; means a day on which (i)&nbsp;trading in the Common
Stock (or other security for which a closing sale price must be determined) generally occurs on The Nasdaq Global Select Market or, if the Common Stock (or such other security) is not then listed on The Nasdaq Global Select Market, on the principal
other U.S. national or regional securities exchange on which the Common Stock (or such other security) is then listed or, if the Common Stock (or such other security) is not then listed on a U.S. national or regional securities exchange, on the
principal other market on which the Common Stock (or such other security) is then traded and (ii)&nbsp;a last reported sale price for the Common Stock (or closing sale price for such other security) is available on such securities exchange or
market; provided that if the Common Stock (or such other security) is not so listed or traded, &#147;Trading Day&#148; means a Business Day. </P>
